</div>
<script>
(function(){
  const c = document.currentScript.closest('.tm-mercarilist-container');
  const loader = c.querySelector('.tm-loader');
  const input = c.querySelector('.tm-search');
  const exclInput = c.querySelector('.tm-exclude-input');
  const items = c.querySelectorAll('.tm-item');

  setTimeout(() => {
    loader.style.display = 'none';
    input.style.display = 'block';
    exclInput.style.display = 'block';
    c.querySelectorAll('.tm-keywords').forEach(box => box.style.display = 'block');
    c.querySelector('.tm-items').style.display = 'grid';
    filter(); // 初期表示でフィルタリング
  }, 300);

  const parseExcludeInput = () => {
    return exclInput.value.toLowerCase().split(/[\s,]+/).filter(Boolean);
  };

  const filter = () => {
    const inputWords = input.value.toLowerCase().split(/\s+/).filter(Boolean);
    const btnInc = Array.from(c.querySelectorAll('.tm-kw.selected')).map(e => e.dataset.kw.toLowerCase());
    const btnExc = Array.from(c.querySelectorAll('.tm-kw-exclude.selected')).map(e => e.dataset.kw.toLowerCase());
    const textExc = parseExcludeInput();

    const allInc = [...inputWords, ...btnInc];
    const allExc = [...btnExc, ...textExc];

    items.forEach(el => {
      const txt = el.dataset.title;
      const okInc = allInc.length ? allInc.some(w => txt.includes(w)) : true;
      const okExc = allExc.every(w => !txt.includes(w));
      el.style.display = (okInc && okExc) ? 'block' : 'none';
    });
  };

  input.addEventListener('input', filter);
  exclInput.addEventListener('input', filter);

  c.querySelectorAll('.tm-kw').forEach(k => {
    k.addEventListener('click', e => {
      e.target.classList.toggle('selected');
      filter();
    });
  });
  c.querySelectorAll('.tm-kw-exclude').forEach(k => {
    k.addEventListener('click', e => {
      e.target.classList.toggle('selected');
      filter();
    });
  });
})();
</script>
</div><script>
    document.querySelectorAll('.kw-grp-btn').forEach(btn => {
      btn.addEventListener('click', e => {
        const grp = e.target.getAttribute('data-group');
        document.querySelectorAll('.kw-grp-btn').forEach(b => b.classList.remove('active'));
        e.target.classList.add('active');
        document.querySelectorAll('.tm-kw-group').forEach(gd => {
          gd.style.display = (gd.getAttribute('data-group') === grp) ? '' : 'none';
          const prodList = gd.querySelector('.product-list');
          if (prodList) prodList.style.display = 'none';
        });
      });
    });
    document.querySelectorAll('.tm-kw-group .tm-kw').forEach(kwEl => {
      kwEl.addEventListener('click', e => {
        const kw = e.target.getAttribute('data-kw') || e.target.textContent.trim();
        const groupDiv = e.target.closest('.tm-kw-group');
        const prodListDiv = groupDiv.querySelector('.product-list');
        let prodData = e.target.getAttribute('data-products');
        if (prodData) {
          try {
            const prods = JSON.parse(prodData);
            let html = '';
            prods.forEach(p => {
              html += '<div class="product-item"><a href="'+p.url+'" target="_blank">'+p.name+'</a></div>';
            });
            prodListDiv.innerHTML = html;
            prodListDiv.style.display = '';
          } catch(err) {
            prodListDiv.style.display = 'none';
          }
        } else {
          prodListDiv.style.display = 'none';
        }
      });
    });
    const firstBtn = document.querySelector('.kw-grp-btn');
    if (firstBtn) firstBtn.classList.add('active');
  </script></body></html>
